Using Chess Servers, you can challenge and play against others or other computer chess programs without the hassle of using a difficult user interface that characterizes most Chess Servers. \r\n\r\nIncluded are the timeseal and timestamp program's which are used with the Chess Servers to compensate for 'net lag' Now you never have to loose a game on time !\r\n\r\nEnhanced Opening book Manager\r\nCan manage up to 8 opening books in parallel. Includes strong learning algorithms.
